 									-
 									<% _.each(tour.duration, function(duration, i) { %>
 										<% if (i) { %>,<% } %>
 										<%- duration.value %>
 									<% }) %>
 									dagen 
 								<% } %>
 								</span>
 								
 							</div>

 							</div>

 									</div>
 								<% } %>
 							<% }) %>
 							
 							<div class="tourDescription">
 								
 								<%- truncateDescriptionText(tour.description) %>
 							</div>

 								<%- tour.description %>
 							</div>
 						</div>

 									<div class="col-xs-7">

 											<a class="infoBtn tourBtn bgAccentGradient" target="_blank" href="/out/<%- tour.id%>" onclick="if (!confirmCookieConsent(this)) { return false } else { ga('send','event', 'affiliate links', '<%- tour.operator.name.replace(/[']/g, "") %>', '<%- tour.id %>')}">meer weten? klik hier</a>
 										<% } %>
 										</div>
 									</div>
 									<div class="col-xs-1">
 									
 									</div>

 										</div>

 				</div>

 		</div>
 	<% }) %>

 	<% if (typeof(nav) != 'undefined') { %>

 						<% } %>
 						<%- nav.start + 1 %> - <%- ((nav.start + nav.perpage) > nav.total) ? nav.total : (nav.start + nav.perpage) %> van <%- nav.total %>
 						<% if (searchResults.nav.hasNext()) { %>

         <script>
          // show large image as background-image
 jQuery(window).load(function(){
 	tourListLayout();
 });
 
 jQuery(window).resize(function(){
 	tourListLayout();
 });
 
 function tourListLayout() {
 
 	// set large image as background image
 	jQuery('.largeImageContainer').each(function(){
 		if (jQuery(this).parent().css('background-image') == 'none') {
 			jQuery(this).parent().css('background-image', 'url('+jQuery(this).find('.imageContainer img').attr('src')+')');
 		}
 		jQuery(this).css('background-image', jQuery(this).first('img').attr('src'));
 		jQuery(this).first('img').css('visibility','hidden')
 	});
 
 }
 
 function scrollToSearchform() {
 	 jQuery('html, body').animate({
         scrollTop: jQuery("#searchFormContainer").parent().offset().top
     }, 500);
 }
 
 function truncateDescriptionText(text) {
 
 	var page = "home";
 	
 	switch (page) {
 		case 'home':
 			if (jQuery("#largeDevice").css("display") == "block") {
 				var truncateLength = 500;
 				break;
 			}
 		default:
 			var truncateLength = 215;
 	}
 	var truncateString = "...";
 	
 	if(text.length > (truncateLength+3)) {
 		var trimmed = text.substring(0,truncateLength);
 		return trimmed.substr(0, Math.min(trimmed.length, trimmed.lastIndexOf(" ")))+truncateString; // return whole words
 	} else {
 		return text;
 	}
 	
 }
         </script>

    <script>
     (function(){
 	var firstSlide = true;
   jQuery('.carousel-showmanymoveone .item').each(function(){
     var itemToClone = jQuery(this);
 	
     for (var i=1;i<6;i++) {
       itemToClone = itemToClone.next();
 
       // wrap around if at end of item collection
       if (!itemToClone.length) {
 		  if (!firstSlide) {
 			itemToClone = jQuery(this).siblings(':first');
 		  } else {
 			itemToClone = jQuery(this);
 		  }
         
       }
 		
       // grab item, clone, add marker class, add to collection
       itemToClone.children(':first-child').clone()
         .addClass("cloneditem-"+(i))
         .appendTo(jQuery(this));
     }
 	
 	firstSlide = false;
   });
 }());
 
 jQuery(document).ready(function(){
 	jQuery("#carousel-tilenav").carousel();
 });

    <script>
     jQuery(window).load(function(){
 		categoryLinkHeight();
 		advertisementTitleHeight();
 
 		jQuery.post('/tours/home').done(function (data) {
 			jQuery('#searchResultsContainer').html(
 				_.template(jQuery('#searchResultsContainerTpl').html()) (
 					JSON.parse(data)
 				)
 			);
 			contentColsHeight();
 		});
 	});
 	jQuery(window).resize(function(){
 		categoryLinkHeight();
 		advertisementTitleHeight();
 	});
 	
 	function categoryLinkHeight() {
 	
 		// set categoryLink div to image height
 		var smallestImgHeight = 0;
 		jQuery('.categoryLink').each(function(){
 			if (smallestImgHeight == 0 || smallestImgHeight > jQuery(this).find('.contentImage').height()) smallestImgHeight = jQuery(this).find('.contentImage').height();
 			
 			jQuery(this).find('.imageContainer').css('background-image', 'url("'+jQuery(this).find('.contentImage').attr('src')+'")');
 			
 			// hide image, background image will be more easy to position
 			jQuery(this).find('.contentImage').css('visibility', 'hidden');
 		});
 		if (smallestImgHeight > 0) {
 			jQuery('.categoryLink').height(smallestImgHeight + 'px');
 			jQuery('.categoryLink .imageContainer').height(smallestImgHeight+'px');
 		}
 		// display categoryLinks
 		jQuery('.categoryLinksContainer').css('visibility', 'visible');
 	}
 	
 	function advertisementTitleHeight() {
 		var largestHight = 0;
 		jQuery('.advertisementTitle').each(function(){ console.log(largestHight)
 			if (largestHight == 0 || largestHight < jQuery(this).height()) largestHight = jQuery(this).height();
 		});
 		if (largestHight > 0) {
 			jQuery('.advertisementTitle').height(largestHight + 'px');
 		}
 	}
    </script>
